\hypertarget{over__hinder_8c_source.tex_l00038}{}\hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_a099e0b2335096053558b8814fcedfc33}{00038} uint8\_t \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_a099e0b2335096053558b8814fcedfc33}{Servo\_Load\_Too\_Small}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} ID)
00039 \{
00040     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \hyperlink{over__hinder_8c_a29122f6df4a054b8141015682f877c82}{load} = \hyperlink{servo___u_a_r_t_8c_a1aae94381111766cdccb93eae5b5c382}{Get\_Servo\_Load}(ID);
00041     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(((ID == 3) || (ID == 9) || (ID == 15))) \textcolor{comment}{//testar på de yttre servona }
00042     \{
00043         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(load > 0x0405)
00044         \{
00045             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;
00046         \}
00047         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
00048         \{
00049             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;
00050         \}
00051     \}
00052     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{comment}{// dvs ID = 4, 10, 16...//testar på de yttre servona }
00053     \{
00054         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((load > 0x0028) && (load < 0x0400)) 
00055         \{
00056             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;
00057         \}
00058         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
00059         \{
00060             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;
00061         \}
00062     \}
00063 \}
